<p>Andhra Pradesh's economy is mainly based on agriculture and livestock. Four important rivers of India, the <a href="/wiki/Godavari_River" title="Godavari River">Godavari</a>, <a href="/wiki/Krishna_River" title="Krishna River">Krishna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penner_River" class="mw-redirect" title="Penner River">Penna</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tungabhadra_River" title="Tungabhadra River">Thungabhadra</a> flow through the state and provide irrigation. 60 percent of the population is engaged in agriculture and related activities. Rice is the major food crop and staple food of the state. It is an exporter of many agricultural products and is also known as "Rice Bowl of India".<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-rice_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rice-97">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> The state has three Agricultural Economic Zones in Chittoor district for mango pulp and vegetables, Krishna district for mangoes, Guntur district for chilies.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Besides rice, farmers also grow jowar, bajra, maize, minor millet, coarse grain, many varieties of pulses, oil seeds, <a href="/wiki/Sugarcane" title="Sugarcane">sugarcane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cotton" title="Cotton">cotton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chili_pepper" title="Chili pepper">chili pepper</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mango" title="Mango">mango</a> nuts and tobacco. Crops used for vegetable oil production such as <a href="/wiki/Sunflower" class="mw-redirect" title="Sunflower">sunflower</a> and peanuts are popular. There are many multi-state irrigation projects under development, including <a href="/wiki/Godavari_River_Basin_Irrigation_Projects" title="Godavari River Basin Irrigation Projects">Godavari River Basin Irrigation Projects</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nagarjuna_Sagar_Dam" title="Nagarjuna Sagar Dam">Nagarjuna Sagar Dam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-irrigation_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-irrigation-99">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Livestock and poultry is also another profitable business, which involves rearing cattle in enclosed areas for commercial purposes. The state is also a largest producer of eggs in the country and hence, it is nicknamed as "<i>Egg Bowl of Asia"</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-egg_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-egg-101">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Fisheries contribute 10% of total fish and over 70% of the shrimp production<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> of India. The geographical location of the state allows marine fishing as well as inland fish production. The most exported marine exports include <i><a href="/wiki/Whiteleg_shrimp" title="Whiteleg shrimp">Vannamei shrimp</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> and are expected to cross  billion in 2013–2014.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Infrastructure">Infrastructure</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Infrastructure">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Andhra Pradesh is investing in building infrastructure in the state such as highways and making every service of the government digital.<a href="/wiki/National_Highway_16_(India)" title="National Highway 16 (India)">National Highway 16 (India)</a> passes through Andhra Pradesh. The <a href="/wiki/List_of_state_highways_in_Andhra_Pradesh" title="List of state highways in Andhra Pradesh">highways in the state</a> are also being widened. <a href="/wiki/APSFL" class="mw-redirect" title="APSFL">APSFL</a> is an initiative of the government of Andhra Pradesh to set up an optical fiber network throughout the thirteen districts of Andhra Pradesh. This network provides internet connectivity, telephony and <a href="/wiki/IPTV" class="mw-redirect" title="IPTV">IPTV</a> with fiber to private and corporate users of Andhra Pradesh.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> The state also has seaports such as <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_Port" title="Visakhapatnam Port">Visakhapatnam Port</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kakinada_Port" title="Kakinada Port">Kakinada Port</a>, <a href="/wiki/Krishnapatnam_Port" title="Krishnapatnam Port">Krishnapatnam Port</a> for import and export and a shipyard for building ships at Visakhapatnam. Major airports in the state are <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rajamahendravaram" class="mw-redirect" title="Rajamahendravaram">Rajamahendravaram</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a> and Tirupati with <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_Airport" title="Visakhapatnam Airport">Visakhapatnam</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Tirupati_airport&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tirupati airport (page does not exist)">Tirupati</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada_Airport" title="Vijayawada Airport">Vijayawada</a> being international airports.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Industrial_sector">Industrial sector</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Industrial sector">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Front of large round building, with street and trees in front" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg/220px-Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg/330px-Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg/440px-Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Satyam_campus_in_Visakhapatnam.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Tech_Mahindra" title="Tech Mahindra">Tech Mahindra</a> Development Centre, <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a></div></div></div>
<p>The industrial sector of the state includes some of the key sectors like <a href="/wiki/Pharmaceutical_industry" title="Pharmaceutical industry">pharmaceutica</a>l, <a href="/wiki/Automobile_industry" class="mw-redirect" title="Automobile industry">automobile</a>, <a href="/wiki/Textile_industry_in_India" title="Textile industry in India">textiles</a> etc. <a href="/wiki/Sricity" class="mw-redirect" title="Sricity">Sricity</a> located in <a href="/wiki/Chittoor_district" title="Chittoor district">Chittoor district</a> is an integrated business city which is home to  firms including <a href="/wiki/PepsiCo" title="PepsiCo">PepsiCo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Isuzu_Motors" title="Isuzu Motors">Isuzu Motors</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cadbury_India" class="mw-redirect" title="Cadbury India">Cadbury India</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kellogg%27s" title="Kellogg&#39;s">Kellogg's</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colgate-Palmolive" title="Colgate-Palmolive">Colgate-Palmolive</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kobelco" class="mw-redirect" title="Kobelco">Kobelco</a> etc.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/PepsiCo" title="PepsiCo">PepsiCo</a> firm has its largest plant in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> at Sri City.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> The state is also emerging as destination for the automobile industry which already hosts companies including <a href="/wiki/Ashok_Leyland" title="Ashok Leyland">Ashok Leyland</a> in Krishna district, <a href="/wiki/Hero_Motors" title="Hero Motors">Hero Motors</a> in Chittoor district, <a href="/wiki/Kia_Motors" title="Kia Motors">Kia Motors</a> in Anantapur district.
</p><p>The state is also emerging in information technology and biotechnology. The IT/ITES revenues of <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a> is at <span class="nowrap"><span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span>14.45 billion</span> (US$210&#160;million) in 2012–2013. The development of IT in Tier-II and Tier-III cities like <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kakinada" title="Kakinada">Kakinada</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tirupati,_Andhra_Pradesh" class="mw-redirect" title="Tirupati, Andhra Pradesh">Tirupati</a> is also improving. In the fiscal year 2012–2013, Vijayawada's IT/ITeS revenues were <span class="nowrap"><span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span>1,153 million</span> (US$17&#160;million) crore. <a href="/wiki/Tirupati,_Andhra_Pradesh" class="mw-redirect" title="Tirupati, Andhra Pradesh">Tirupati</a> with <span class="nowrap"><span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span>693 million</span> (US$10&#160;million) and <a href="/wiki/Kakinada" title="Kakinada">Kakinada</a> with <span class="nowrap"><span style="white-space: nowrap">₹</span>615 million</span> (US$8.9&#160;million) stand next.<sup id="cite_ref-it_sector_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-it_sector-108">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> For the benefit of state i.e., after separating Telangana from Andhra, people of Andhra protested for special status during January in 2017
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Resources">Resources</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Resources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Andhra Pradesh is one of the storehouses of mineral resources in India. Andhra Pradesh with varied geological formations, contain rich and variety of industrial minerals and building stones.<sup id="cite_ref-minerals_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-minerals-109">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Andhra Pradesh is listed at the top in the deposit and production of mica in India. Minerals found in the state include limestone, reserves of oil and natural gas, manganese, asbestos, iron ore, ball clay, fire clay, gold diamonds, graphite, dolomite, quartz, tungsten, steatitic, feldspar, silica sand. It has about one-third of India's <a href="/wiki/Limestone" title="Limestone">limestone</a> reserves and is known for large exclusive deposits of barytes and galaxy granite in the international market.<sup id="cite_ref-minerals_109-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-minerals-109">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mining">Mining</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Mining">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Mining is identified as one of the growth engines for the overall development of industry and infrastructure. The <a href="/wiki/Tummalapalle_Uranium_mine" class="mw-redirect" title="Tummalapalle Uranium mine">Tummalapalle Uranium mine</a> in Andhra has confirmed 49,000 tonnes of ore and there are indications that it could hold reserves totaling three times its current size. 700 million tonnes of metal grade Bauxite deposits in proximity to <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_Port" title="Visakhapatnam Port">Visakhapatnam Port</a>.
</p><p>Reliance Industries Limited struck nine trillion cubic feet of gas reserves in the <a href="/wiki/Krishna_Godavari_Basin" title="Krishna Godavari Basin">KG basin</a>, 150&#160;km (93&#160;mi) off the Andhra Pradesh coast near <a href="/wiki/Kakinada" title="Kakinada">Kakinada</a>. Discovery of a large quantity of natural gas in KG Basin is expected to provide rapid economic growth.<sup id="cite_ref-kg_basin_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kg_basin-110">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> During 2016, nearly 134 trillion cubic feet of <a href="/wiki/Methane_clathrate" title="Methane clathrate">methane hydrate</a> deposits were explored in KG basin whose extraction was adequate to impart <a href="/wiki/Energy_security" title="Energy security">energy security</a> for many decades to India.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Power_plants">Power plants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Power plants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Power_sector_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Power sector of Andhra Pradesh">Power sector of Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg/220px-Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="80" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg/330px-Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg/440px-Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1749" data-file-height="633" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rayalaseema Thermal Power Station</div></div></div>
<p>The state is a pioneer nationwide in <a href="/wiki/Solar_power_in_India" title="Solar power in India">solar power generation</a>. <a href="/wiki/APGENCO" class="mw-redirect" title="APGENCO">APGENCO</a> is the power generating company owned by the state.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> The state has become power surplus with excess power generation being exported to other states.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Thermal (natural gas and coal based) and <a href="/wiki/Renewable_power" class="mw-redirect" title="Renewable power">renewable power</a> plants totalling to 21,000 MW were installed in the state by the year 2015. Local power plants of 9,600&#160;<a href="/wiki/Megawatt" class="mw-redirect" title="Megawatt">MW</a> capacity only are supplying electricity in the state which includes <a href="/wiki/Simhadri_Super_Thermal_Power_Plant" class="mw-redirect" title="Simhadri Super Thermal Power Plant">Simhadri Super Thermal Power Plant</a> (2000 MW) of <a href="/wiki/NTPC_Limited" title="NTPC Limited">NTPC</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vizag_Thermal_Power_Station" title="Vizag Thermal Power Station">Vizag Thermal Power Station</a> (1040 MW), <a href="/wiki/Rayalaseema_Thermal_Power_Station" title="Rayalaseema Thermal Power Station">Rayalaseema Thermal Power Station</a> (1650 MW), <a href="/wiki/Sri_Damodaram_Sanjeevaiah_Thermal_Power_Station" title="Sri Damodaram Sanjeevaiah Thermal Power Station">Sri Damodaram Sanjeevaiah Thermal Power Station</a> (1600 MW), <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada_Thermal_Power_Plant" class="mw-redirect" title="Vijayawada Thermal Power Plant">Vijayawada Thermal Power Plant</a> (1760 MW), etc. Hydel power plants have a capacity of 1671 MW.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Culture of Andhra Pradesh">Culture of Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<p>Andhra Pradesh has rich culture and heritage.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kuchipudi" title="Kuchipudi">Kuchipudi</a>, the state dance originated in the village of <a href="/wiki/Kuchipudi,_Krishna_district" title="Kuchipudi, Krishna district">Kuchipudi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Krishna_district" title="Krishna district">Krishna district</a>, had entered the <a href="/wiki/Guinness_World_Records" title="Guinness World Records">Guinness World Records</a> for performing <i>Mahabrinda Natyam</i> with a total of 6,117
dancers in <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> It had thirteen <a href="/wiki/Geographical_indications" class="mw-redirect" title="Geographical indications">geographical indications</a> in categories of <a href="/wiki/Agricultural" class="mw-redirect" title="Agricultural">agricultural</a> <a href="/wiki/Handicraft" title="Handicraft">handicrafts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Foodstuff" class="mw-redirect" title="Foodstuff">foodstuff</a> and <a href="/wiki/Textile" title="Textile">textiles</a> as per <i>Geographical Indications of Goods (Registration and Protection) Act, 1999</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-GIlist_117-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GIlist-117">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> It increased to fifteen with the addition of <a href="/wiki/Banaganapalle_Mangoes" class="mw-redirect" title="Banaganapalle Mangoes">Banaganapalle Mangoes</a><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Bandar_laddu" title="Bandar laddu">Bandar laddu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> The other GI tagged goods are, <a href="/wiki/Bobbili_Veena" title="Bobbili Veena">Bobbili Veena</a>, <a href="/wiki/Budithi_Bell_and_Brass_Craft" title="Budithi Bell and Brass Craft">Budithi Bell and Brass Craft</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dharmavaram_Handloom_Pattu_Sarees_and_Paavadas" class="mw-redirect" title="Dharmavaram Handloom Pattu Sarees and Paavadas">Dharmavaram Handloom Pattu Sarees and Paavadas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guntur_Sannam" title="Guntur Sannam">Guntur Sannam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kondapalli_Toys" title="Kondapalli Toys">Kondapalli Toys</a>, <a href="/wiki/Machilipatnam_Kalamkari" class="mw-redirect" title="Machilipatnam Kalamkari">Machilipatnam Kalamkari</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mangalagiri_Sarees_and_Fabrics" title="Mangalagiri Sarees and Fabrics">Mangalagiri Sarees and Fabrics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Srikalahasti_Kalamkari" title="Srikalahasti Kalamkari">Srikalahasti Kalamkari</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tirupati_Laddu" title="Tirupati Laddu">Tirupati Laddu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uppada_Jamdani_Sari" title="Uppada Jamdani Sari">Uppada Jamdani Sari</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venkatagiri_Sari" title="Venkatagiri Sari">Venkatagiri Sari</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GIlist_117-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GIlist-117">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Arts.2C_crafts_and_artifacts"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Arts,_crafts_and_artifacts">Arts, crafts and artifacts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Arts, crafts and artifacts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg/220px-Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg/330px-Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg/440px-Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kondapalli_toys_at_a_house_in_Vijayawada.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Kondapalli_Toys" title="Kondapalli Toys">Kondapalli Toys</a> at a house in Vijayawada</div></div></div>
<p>Machilipatnam and Srikalahasti Kalamkari are the two unique textile art forms practised in India.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> There are also other notable handicrafts present in the state, like the soft <a href="/wiki/Limestone" title="Limestone">limestone</a> <a href="/wiki/Cult_image" title="Cult image">idol</a> carvings of <a href="/wiki/Durgi" title="Durgi">Durgi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Etikoppaka" title="Etikoppaka">Etikoppaka</a> in <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_district" title="Visakhapatnam district">Visakhapatnam district</a> is notable for its <a href="/wiki/Lac" title="Lac">lac</a> industry, producing lacquered wooden.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The state has many museums, which features a varied collection of ancient sculptures, paintings, idols, weapons, cutlery and inscriptions, and religious artifacts such as the <a href="/wiki/Amaravati_Archaeological_Museum" class="mw-redirect" title="Amaravati Archaeological Museum">Amaravati Archaeological Museum</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Visakha_Museum" title="Visakha Museum">Visakha Museum</a> and <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Culture of Andhra Pradesh">Telugu Cultural Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a> displays the history of the pre-independence and the <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Jubilee_Museum" class="mw-redirect" title="Victoria Jubilee Museum">Victoria Jubilee Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a> with large collection of artifacts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Literature">Literature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Literature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Telugu_literature" title="Telugu literature">Telugu literature</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Nannayya" title="Nannayya">Nannayya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tikkana" title="Tikkana">Tikkana</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yerrapragada" title="Yerrapragada">Yerrapragada</a> form the trinity who translated the <a href="/wiki/Sanskrit" title="Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a> epic <i><a href="/wiki/Mahabharata" title="Mahabharata">Mahabharata</a></i> into <a href="/wiki/Telugu_language" title="Telugu language">Telugu language</a>. Nannayya wrote the first treatise on Telugu grammar called <i>Andhra Shabda Chintamani</i> in Sanskrit, as there was no grammatical work in Telugu prior to that.<sup id="cite_ref-Padmapriya_ch1_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Padmapriya_ch1-125">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pothana" title="Pothana">Pothana</a> is the poet who composed the classic <i>Srimad Maha Bhagavatamu</i>, a Telugu translation of <i>Sri Bhagavatam</i>. <a href="/wiki/Vemana" title="Vemana">Vemana</a> is notable for his philosophical poems. The <a href="/wiki/Vijayanagara" title="Vijayanagara">Vijayanagara</a> emperor <a href="/wiki/Krishnadevaraya" title="Krishnadevaraya">Krishnadevaraya</a> wrote <a href="/wiki/Amuktamalyada" title="Amuktamalyada">Amuktamalyada</a>. Telugu literature after <a href="/wiki/Kandukuri_Veeresalingam" title="Kandukuri Veeresalingam">Kandukuri Veeresalingam</a> is termed as Adhunika Telugu Sahityam (Modern Telugu literature). He is known as <i>Gadya Tikkana</i> and was the author of Telugu <a href="/wiki/Social_novel" title="Social novel">social novel</a>, <i>Satyavati Charitam</i>. <a href="/wiki/Jnanpith_Award" title="Jnanpith Award">Jnanpith Award</a> holders from the state include <a href="/wiki/Viswanatha_Satyanarayana" title="Viswanatha Satyanarayana">Viswanatha Satyanarayana</a>. The Andhra Pradesh native and revolutionary poet <a href="/wiki/Srirangam_Srinivasarao" class="mw-redirect" title="Srirangam Srinivasarao">Sri Sri</a> brought new forms of expressionism into Telugu literature.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Art_and_cinema">Art and cinema</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Art and cinema">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Music of Andhra Pradesh">Music of Andhra Pradesh</a> and <a href="/wiki/Telugu_theatre" class="mw-redirect" title="Telugu theatre">Telugu theatre</a></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Tholu_bommalata" title="Tholu bommalata">Tholu bommalata</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg/170px-Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="256" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg/255px-Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg/340px-Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="6016" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Prathiksha_Kashi.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Kuchipudi" title="Kuchipudi">Kuchipudi</a> dance</div></div></div>
<p>Many composers of <a href="/wiki/Carnatic_music" title="Carnatic music">Carnatic music</a> like <a href="/wiki/Annamacharya" title="Annamacharya">Annamacharya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kshetrayya" title="Kshetrayya">Kshetrayya</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bhadrachala_Ramadas" class="mw-redirect" title="Bhadrachala Ramadas">Bhadrachala Ramadas</a> were of Telugu descent. Modern Carnatic music composers and singers like <a href="/wiki/Ghantasala_(singer)" title="Ghantasala (singer)">Ghantasala</a>, Sujatha Puligella and <a href="/wiki/M._Balamuralikrishna" title="M. Balamuralikrishna">M. Balamuralikrishna</a> are also of Telugu descent. The Telugu film industry hosts many music composers and playback singers such as <a href="/wiki/S._P._Balasubrahmanyam" title="S. P. Balasubrahmanyam">S. P. Balasubrahmanyam</a>, <a href="/wiki/P._Susheela" title="P. Susheela">P. Susheela</a>, <a href="/wiki/S._Janaki" title="S. Janaki">S. Janaki</a> and <a href="/wiki/P._B._Sreenivas" title="P. B. Sreenivas">P. B. Sreenivas</a>. Folk songs are very important and popular in the many rural areas of the state. Forms such as the <i><a href="/wiki/Burra_katha" title="Burra katha">Burra katha</a></i> and <i>Poli</i> are still performed today.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> <i>Harikathaa Kalakshepam (or Harikatha)</i> involves the narration of a story, intermingled with various songs relating to the story. Harikatha was originated in Andhra.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> <i>Burra katha</i> is an <a href="/wiki/Oral_storytelling" title="Oral storytelling">oral storytelling</a> technique with the topic be either a <a href="/wiki/Hindu" class="mw-redirect" title="Hindu">Hindu</a> mythological story or a contemporary social issue.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> <i>Rangasthalam</i> is an <a href="/wiki/Theatre_of_India" title="Theatre of India">Indian theatre</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Telugu_language" title="Telugu language">Telugu language</a>, based predominantly in Andhra Pradesh.<sup id="cite_ref-auto5_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto5-130">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Gurazada_Apparao" title="Gurazada Apparao">Gurazada Apparao</a> wrote the play <i><a href="/wiki/Kanyasulkam" title="Kanyasulkam">Kanyasulkam</a></i> in 1892, often considered the greatest play in the Telugu language.<sup id="cite_ref-auto3_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto3-131">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/C._Pullaiah" title="C. Pullaiah">C. Pullaiah</a> is cited as the father of Telugu <a href="/wiki/Theatre" title="Theatre">theatre</a> movement.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SoManyCinemas_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SoManyCinemas-133">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Telugu film industry is largely based in <a href="/wiki/Hyderabad" title="Hyderabad">Hyderabad</a> and <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a>. The Telugu film culture (also known as "<a href="/wiki/Telugu_cinema" title="Telugu cinema">Tollywood</a>") is the second-largest film industry in India next to the <a href="/wiki/Bollywood" title="Bollywood">Bollywood</a> film industry.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Film producer <a href="/wiki/D._Ramanaidu" title="D. Ramanaidu">D. Ramanaidu</a> holds a <a href="/wiki/Guinness_Record" class="mw-redirect" title="Guinness Record">Guinness Record</a> for the most films produced by a person.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> In the years 2005, 2006 and 2008, the Telugu film industry produced the largest number of films in India, exceeding the number of films produced in Bollywood.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> The industry holds the Guinness World Record for the largest film production facility in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg/220px-Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg/330px-Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg/440px-Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3008" data-file-height="2000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vegetarian_Andhra_Meal.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Vegetarian Andhra meal, served on important occasions</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Telugu_cuisine" title="Telugu cuisine">Telugu cuisine</a></div>
<p>Telugu people's traditional sweet <a href="/wiki/Pootharekulu" title="Pootharekulu">Pootharekulu</a> originated from Atreyapuram village, Andhra Pradesh.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">Tourism</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Tourism">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tourism_in_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Tourism in Andhra Pradesh">Tourism in Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg/220px-Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg/330px-Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg/440px-Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4288" data-file-height="2848" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ananta_Padmanabha_Swami_Temple.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Undavalli_Caves" title="Undavalli Caves">Undavalli Caves</a>, is a <a href="/wiki/Monolithic_architecture" title="Monolithic architecture">monolithic</a> example of <a href="/wiki/Indian_rock-cut_architecture" title="Indian rock-cut architecture">Indian rock-cut architecture</a> and one of the finest testimonials to ancient <i>viswakarma sthapathis</i>.</div></div></div>
<p>The state has several beaches in its coastal districts such as, Rushikonda, Mypadu, Suryalanka etc.;<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> caves such as, <a href="/wiki/Borra_Caves" title="Borra Caves">Borra Caves</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Indian_rock-cut_architecture" title="Indian rock-cut architecture">Indian rock-cut architecture</a> depicting <a href="/wiki/Undavalli_caves" class="mw-redirect" title="Undavalli caves">Undavalli caves</a><sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> and the country's second longest caves- the <a href="/wiki/Belum_Caves" title="Belum Caves">Belum Caves</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> The valleys and hills include, <a href="/wiki/Araku_Valley" title="Araku Valley">Araku Valley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Horsley_Hills" title="Horsley Hills">Horsley Hills</a>, <a href="/wiki/Papi_Hills" class="mw-redirect" title="Papi Hills">Papi Hills</a> etc.<sup id="cite_ref-aptdc_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aptdc-143">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Arma_Konda" title="Arma Konda">Arma Konda</a> peak located in Visakhapatnam district is the highest peak in <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Ghats" title="Eastern Ghats">Eastern Ghats</a>.
</p><p>The state is home to various religious pilgrim destinations such as, <a href="/wiki/Tirumala_Temple" class="mw-redirect" title="Tirumala Temple">Tirumala Temple</a>, <a href="/wiki/Simhachalam_Temple" class="mw-redirect" title="Simhachalam Temple">Simhachalam Temple</a>, <a href="/wiki/Annavaram" title="Annavaram">Annavaram</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mallikarjuna_Swamy" class="mw-redirect" title="Mallikarjuna Swamy">Srisailam temple</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kanaka_Durga_Temple" title="Kanaka Durga Temple">Kanaka Durga Temple</a>, <a href="/wiki/Amaralingeswara_Swamy" class="mw-redirect" title="Amaralingeswara Swamy">Amaravati</a>, <a href="/wiki/Srikalahasti" title="Srikalahasti">Srikalahasti</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shahi_jamia_masjid" class="mw-redirect" title="Shahi jamia masjid">Shahi jamia masjid</a> in <a href="/wiki/Adoni" title="Adoni">Adoni</a>, Gunadala Church in <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a>, Buddhist centres at <a href="/wiki/Amaravathi_village,_Guntur_district" class="mw-redirect" title="Amaravathi village, Guntur district">Amaravati</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nagarjuna_Konda" class="mw-redirect" title="Nagarjuna Konda">Nagarjuna Konda</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> and many more as well.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">Transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The state is well connected to other states through road and rail networks. It is also connected to other countries by means of airways and seaports as well. With a long seacoast along the <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Bengal" title="Bay of Bengal">Bay of Bengal</a>, it also has many ports for sea trade. The state has one of the largest railway junctions at Vijayawada and one of the largest seaports at Visakhapatnam.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Roads">Roads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Roads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Rps20160709_141628.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Rps20160709_141628.jpg/220px-Rps20160709_141628.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="103" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Rps20160709_141628.jpg/330px-Rps20160709_141628.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Rps20160709_141628.jpg/440px-Rps20160709_141628.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="705" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Rps20160709_141628.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a>-<a href="/wiki/Guntur" title="Guntur">Guntur</a> Expressway section of NH-16</div></div></div>
<p>The state has a total road network of 53,403&#160;km (33,183&#160;mi), of which 6,401&#160;km (3,977&#160;mi) of <a href="/wiki/National_Highway_(India)" title="National Highway (India)">National highways</a>, 14,722&#160;km (9,148&#160;mi) of <a href="/wiki/State_highways" class="mw-redirect" title="State highways">state highways</a> and 32,280&#160;km (20,060&#160;mi) of district roads.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/National_Highway_5_(India)(old_numbering)" class="mw-redirect" title="National Highway 5 (India)(old numbering)">NH 16</a>, with a highway network of around 1,000&#160;km (620&#160;mi) in the state, is a part of <a href="/wiki/Golden_Quadrilateral_Project" class="mw-redirect" title="Golden Quadrilateral Project">Golden Quadrilateral Project</a> undertaken by <a href="/wiki/National_Highways_Development_Project" title="National Highways Development Project">National Highways Development Project</a>. It also forms part of <a href="/wiki/Asian_Highway" class="mw-redirect" title="Asian Highway">AH 45</a> which comes under the <a href="/wiki/Asian_Highway_Network" title="Asian Highway Network">Asian Highway Network</a>.
</p><p>The state government owned <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh_State_Road_Transport_Corporation" title="Andhra Pradesh State Road Transport Corporation">Andhra Pradesh State Road Transport Corporation</a> (APSRTC) is the major public bus transport, which runs thousands of buses connecting different parts of the state. <a href="/wiki/Pandit_Nehru_Bus_Station" class="mw-redirect" title="Pandit Nehru Bus Station">Pandit Nehru Bus Station</a> (PNBS) in <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada" title="Vijayawada">Vijayawada</a> is one of the largest bus terminals in <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> From 30 January 2019, all the vehicles in the state are registered as <a href="/wiki/List_of_RTO_districts_in_India" class="mw-redirect" title="List of RTO districts in India">AP–39</a>, followed by an alphabet and four digits.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Railways">Railways</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Railways">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/South_Coast_Railway_zone" title="South Coast Railway zone">South Coast Railway zone</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg/220px-VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg/330px-VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg/440px-VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1152" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:VijayawadaRailwayStation.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vijayawada_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Vijayawada railway station">Vijayawada railway station</a></div></div></div><p>Andhra Pradesh <sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> has a total <a href="/wiki/Broad_gauge" class="mw-redirect" title="Broad gauge">broad gauge</a> railway route of 3703.25&#160;km and has no <a href="/wiki/Metre_gauge_railway" class="mw-redirect" title="Metre gauge railway">metre gauge</a> railway.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> The rail density of the state is 16.59 per 1,000&#160;km (620&#160;mi), compared to an all India average of 20.<sup id="cite_ref-apedb_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-apedb-150">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Howrah%E2%80%93Chennai_main_line" title="Howrah–Chennai main line">Howrah–Chennai main line</a> which runs through the state is proposed to be upgraded into a high-speed rail corridor through the <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Quadrilateral" title="Diamond Quadrilateral">Diamond Quadrilateral</a> project of the Indian Railways.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The railway network spans two <a href="/wiki/Zones_and_divisions_of_Indian_Railways" title="Zones and divisions of Indian Railways">zones</a>, further subdivided into divisions – <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada_railway_division" title="Vijayawada railway division">Vijayawada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guntur_railway_division" title="Guntur railway division">Guntur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Guntakal_railway_division" title="Guntakal railway division">Guntakal railway divisions</a> of <a href="/wiki/South_Central_Railway_zone" title="South Central Railway zone">South Central Railway zone</a>.,<sup id="cite_ref-scr_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scr-153">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Waltair_railway_division" title="Waltair railway division">Waltair railway division</a> of <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_Railway_zone" title="East Coast Railway zone">East Coast Railway zone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> There is a demand for creating a unified zone for the state based out of <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a>.
</p><p>There are three A1 and twenty three A-category railway stations in the state.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_railway_station" title="Visakhapatnam railway station">Visakhapatnam railway station</a> has been declared the cleanest railway station in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> The railway station of <a href="/wiki/Shimiliguda" title="Shimiliguda">Shimiliguda</a> was the first highest <a href="/wiki/Broad_gauge" class="mw-redirect" title="Broad gauge">broad gauge</a> railway station in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Airports">Airports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Airports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Andhra_Pradesh" title="List of airports in Andhra Pradesh">List of airports in Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/220px-Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="210" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/330px-Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/440px-Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 2x" data-file-width="909" data-file-height="867" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_Airports_and_airstrips_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of airports and airstrips of Andhra Pradesh</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_Airport" title="Visakhapatnam Airport">Visakhapatnam Airport</a>, is the only airport in the state with operating international flights while <a href="/wiki/Vijayawada_Airport" title="Vijayawada Airport">Vijayawada Airport</a> at Gannavaram has launched an international flight to <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>, recently.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> The state has four other <a href="/wiki/Domestic_airports" class="mw-redirect" title="Domestic airports">domestic airports</a>,  <a href="/wiki/Rajahmundry_Airport" title="Rajahmundry Airport">Rajahmundry Airport</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuddapah_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Cuddapah Airport">Cuddapah Airport</a>, a privately owned, public use airport at <a href="/wiki/Sri_Sathya_Sai_Airport" title="Sri Sathya Sai Airport">Puttaparthi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tirupati_Airport" title="Tirupati Airport">Tirupati Airport</a> located in the city of <a href="/wiki/Tirupati" title="Tirupati">Tirupati</a>. There are also 16 small air strips located in the state.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/220px-Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="210" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/330px-Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/440px-Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 2x" data-file-width="923" data-file-height="881" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Seaports_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of seaports in Andhra Pradesh<br /> (click on the image for maximum view)</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sea_ports">Sea ports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Sea ports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Ports_and_harbours_of_Andhra_Pradesh" class="mw-redirect" title="Ports and harbours of Andhra Pradesh">Ports and harbours of Andhra Pradesh</a></div><p>Andhra Pradesh has one of the country's largest port at <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam_Port" title="Visakhapatnam Port">Visakhapatnam</a> in terms of cargo handling.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> The other famous ports are <a href="/wiki/Krishnapatnam_Port" title="Krishnapatnam Port">Krishnapatnam Port</a> (<a href="/wiki/Nellore_district" title="Nellore district">Nellore</a>), <a href="/wiki/Gangavaram_Port" title="Gangavaram Port">Gangavaram Port</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kakinada_Port" title="Kakinada Port">Kakinada Port</a>. <a href="/wiki/Gangavaram_Port" title="Gangavaram Port">Gangavaram Port</a> is a deep seaport which can accommodate ocean liners up to 200,000–250,000 <a href="/wiki/Deadweight_tonnage" title="Deadweight tonnage">DWT</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> There are 14 notified non-major ports at Bheemunipatnam, S.Yanam, Machilipatnam, Nizampatnam, and Vadarevu.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup>
</p><h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education_and_research">Education and research</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Education and research">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Education in Andhra Pradesh">Education in Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/220px-Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="210" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/330px-Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png/440px-Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png 2x" data-file-width="923" data-file-height="881" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Universities_Map_of_Andhra_Pradesh.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of universities in Andhra Pradesh</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Guntur-Agri-University.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e3/Guntur-Agri-University.jpg/220px-Guntur-Agri-University.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e3/Guntur-Agri-University.jpg/330px-Guntur-Agri-University.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e3/Guntur-Agri-University.jpg/440px-Guntur-Agri-University.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3856" data-file-height="3022" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Guntur-Agri-University.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Agriculture University, <a href="/wiki/Guntur" title="Guntur">Guntur</a></div></div></div>
<p>Andhra Pradesh has an overall <a href="/wiki/Literacy_rate" class="mw-redirect" title="Literacy rate">literacy rate</a> of 67.41% as per the 2011 Indian census.<sup id="cite_ref-demographics_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-demographics-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Primary_education" title="Primary education">primary</a> and <a href="/wiki/Secondary_education" title="Secondary education">secondary</a> school education is imparted by <a href="/wiki/Government_School" class="mw-redirect" title="Government School">government</a>, aided and <a href="/wiki/Private_schools" class="mw-redirect" title="Private schools">private schools</a>, managed and regulated by the School Education Department of the state.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> There are urban, rural and <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh_Residential_School" class="mw-redirect" title="Andhra Pradesh Residential School">residential schools</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> As per the child info and school information report (2018–19), there were a total of 7,041,568 students,<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> enrolled in 62,063 schools respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Directorate_of_Government_Examinations" title="Directorate of Government Examinations">Directorate of Government Examinations</a> of the state administers and conduct the <a href="/wiki/Secondary_School_Certificate" title="Secondary School Certificate">Secondary School Certificate</a> (SSC) examination.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> More than <span class="nowrap">6 <a href="/wiki/Lakh" title="Lakh">lakh</a></span> students have appeared for the 2019 SSC exam and recorded an overall pass percentage of 94.88% with a 100% pass percentage in 5,464 schools.<sup id="cite_ref-ssc2019_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ssc2019-171">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> The mediums of instruction are primarily <a href="/wiki/Telugu_language" title="Telugu language">Telugu</a> and <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> with a very few opting for <a href="/wiki/Urdu" title="Urdu">Urdu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hindi" title="Hindi">Hindi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kannada_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Kannada language">Kannada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Odia_language" title="Odia language">Odia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tamil_language" title="Tamil language">Tamil</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ssc2015_172-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ssc2015-172">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Higher_education" title="Higher education">Higher education</a> in the state is administered by the Department of Higher Education.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> The central universities are <a href="/wiki/All_India_Institute_of_Medical_Sciences" class="mw-redirect" title="All India Institute of Medical Sciences">All India Institute of Medical Sciences</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Management_Visakhapatnam" title="Indian Institute of Management Visakhapatnam">IIM Visakhapatnam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Technology_Tirupati" title="Indian Institute of Technology Tirupati">IIT Tirupati</a>, <a href="/wiki/National_Institute_of_Technology_Andhra_Pradesh" class="mw-redirect" title="National Institute of Technology Andhra Pradesh">NIT Tadepalligudem</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Information_Technology_Design_and_Manufacturing,_Kurnool" title="Indian Institute of Information Technology Design and Manufacturing, Kurnool">IIITDM Kurnool</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-central_universities_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-central_universities-174">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Petroleum_and_Energy" title="Indian Institute of Petroleum and Energy">Indian Institute of Petroleum and Energy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup><a href="/wiki/National_Institute_of_Design,_Vijayawada" title="National Institute of Design, Vijayawada">NIDV</a>, Central University of Andhra Pradesh, <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Information_Technology,_Sri_City" title="Indian Institute of Information Technology, Sri City">IIIT Sri City</a>, <a href="/wiki/IISER_Tirupati" class="mw-redirect" title="IISER Tirupati">IISER Tirupati</a>, Agriculture University, Guntur and IIFT Kakinada. The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Government of Andhra Pradesh">Government of Andhra Pradesh</a> established Rajiv Gandhi University of Knowledge Technologies (RGUKT) in 2008 to cater to the education needs of the rural youth of Andhra Pradesh.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> As per the University Grants Commission,
<a href="/wiki/Gandhi_Institute_of_Technology_and_Management" title="Gandhi Institute of Technology and Management">GITAM</a>, <a href="/wiki/K_L_University" class="mw-redirect" title="K L University">K L University</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vignan_University" class="mw-redirect" title="Vignan University">Vignan University</a> are the <a href="/wiki/Deemed_Universities" class="mw-redirect" title="Deemed Universities">Deemed Universities</a> in the state.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> There are 18 state universities in the districts providing higher education in <a href="/wiki/Horticulture" title="Horticulture">horticulture</a>, <a href="/wiki/Law" title="Law">law</a>, <a href="/wiki/Medical" class="mw-redirect" title="Medical">medical</a>, <a href="/wiki/Technology" title="Technology">technology</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vedic" class="mw-redirect" title="Vedic">Vedic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Veterinary" class="mw-redirect" title="Veterinary">veterinary</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Andhra_University" title="Andhra University">Andhra University</a> is the oldest of the universities in the state, established in 1926.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Research">Research</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Research">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Research institutes have been set up by the central state government. Naval Science &amp; Technological Laboratory (NSTL), <a href="/wiki/National_Institute_of_Oceanography,_India" title="National Institute of Oceanography, India">National Institute of Oceanography</a>, Visakhapatnam (NIO), <a href="/wiki/School_of_Planning_and_Architecture,_Vijayawada" title="School of Planning and Architecture, Vijayawada">School of Planning and Architecture</a> at Vijayawada is an autonomous research institute under <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Human_Resource_Development" title="Ministry of Human Resource Development">Ministry of Human Resource Development</a> of <a href="/wiki/Government_of_India" title="Government of India">Government of India</a>, <a href="/wiki/National_Atmospheric_Research_Laboratory" title="National Atmospheric Research Laboratory">National Atmospheric Research Laboratory</a> carry out fundamental and applied research in atmospheric and space sciences,<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Indian_Institute_of_Science_Education_and_Research,_Tirupati" title="Indian Institute of Science Education and Research, Tirupati">Indian Institute of Science Education and Research, Tirupati</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> Society for Applied Microwave Electronics Engineering and Research, <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a> Central Tobacco Research Institute, <a href="/wiki/Rajahmundry" title="Rajahmundry">Rajahmundry</a> under control of ICAR (Indian Council of Agriculture Research) conducts fundamental and applied research on tobacco for the benefit of the farming community,<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> Indian Institute of Oil Palm Research (IIOPR) at Pedavegi near <a href="/wiki/Eluru" title="Eluru">Eluru</a> in <a href="/wiki/West_Godavari_district" title="West Godavari district">West Godavari district</a> serves as a centre for conducting and co-ordinating research on all aspects of oil palm conservation, improvement, production, protection, post-harvest technology and transfer of technology,<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> CCRH Regional Research Institute at <a href="/wiki/Gudivada" title="Gudivada">Gudivada</a>, Clinical Research Institute at <a href="/wiki/Tirupati" title="Tirupati">Tirupati</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Institute_of_Oceanography,_India" title="National Institute of Oceanography, India">National Institute of Oceanography</a><sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> at <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a> are some of them.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Space_research_organisation">Space research organisation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Space research organisation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Satish_Dhawan_Space_Centre" title="Satish Dhawan Space Centre">Satish Dhawan Space Centre</a>, also known as Sriharikota Range (SHAR), at barrier island of <a href="/wiki/Sriharikota" title="Sriharikota">Sriharikota</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nellore_district" title="Nellore district">Nellore district</a> of Andhra Pradesh is a satellite launching station operated by <a href="/wiki/Indian_Space_Research_Organisation" title="Indian Space Research Organisation">Indian Space Research Organisation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> It is India's primary orbital launch site. India's lunar orbiter <a href="/wiki/Chandrayaan-1" title="Chandrayaan-1">Chandrayaan-1</a> was launched from the centre at 6:22 <a href="/wiki/Ante_meridiem" class="mw-redirect" title="Ante meridiem">AM</a> <a href="/wiki/Indian_Standard_Time" title="Indian Standard Time">IST</a> on 22 October 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andhra_Pradesh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Andhra_Pradesh" title="Sports in Andhra Pradesh">Sports in Andhra Pradesh</a></div>
<p>The Sports Authority of Andhra Pradesh is the governing body which looks after the infrastructure development in <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">cricket</a>, <a href="/wiki/Field_hockey" title="Field hockey">field hockey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roller_skating" title="Roller skating">Skating</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olympic_weightlifting" title="Olympic weightlifting">Olympic weightlifting</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chess" title="Chess">chess</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water_sports" class="mw-redirect" title="Water sports">water sports</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Badminton" title="Badminton">badminton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Table_tennis" title="Table tennis">table tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cycling" title="Cycling">cycling</a>, etc.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">Cricket</a> is one of the most popular sports in the state. The <a href="/wiki/ACA-VDCA_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="ACA-VDCA Stadium">ACA-VDCA Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Visakhapatnam" title="Visakhapatnam">Visakhapatnam</a> is the home to <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Andhra Pradesh cricket team">Andhra Pradesh cricket team</a>. The venue regularly hosts international as well as domestic matches. Notable cricketers from Andhra Pradesh include  former Indian captain <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Azharuddin" title="Mohammad Azharuddin">Mohammad Azharuddin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maharajkumar_of_Vizianagram" title="Maharajkumar of Vizianagram">Maharajkumar of Vizianagram</a>, <a href="/wiki/M._V._Narasimha_Rao" title="M. V. Narasimha Rao">M. V. Narasimha Rao</a>, <a href="/wiki/M._S._K._Prasad" title="M. S. K. Prasad">M. S. K. Prasad</a>, <a href="/wiki/V._V._S._Laxman" class="mw-redirect" title="V. V. S. Laxman">V. V. S. Laxman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tirumalasetti_Suman" title="Tirumalasetti Suman">Tirumalasetti Suman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arshad_Ayub" title="Arshad Ayub">Arshad Ayub</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ambati_Rayudu" title="Ambati Rayudu">Ambati Rayudu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Venkatapathy_Raju" title="Venkatapathy Raju">Venkatapathy Raju</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sravanthi_Naidu" title="Sravanthi Naidu">Sravanthi Naidu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yalaka_Venugopal_Rao" class="mw-redirect" title="Yalaka Venugopal Rao">Yalaka Venugopal Rao</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hanuma_Vihari" title="Hanuma Vihari">Hanuma Vihari</a>. <a href="/wiki/Humpy_Koneru" title="Humpy Koneru">Humpy Koneru</a>, from <a href="/wiki/Gudivada" title="Gudivada">Gudivada</a> in <a href="/wiki/Krishna_district" title="Krishna district">Krishna district</a>, is an <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Chess" title="Chess">chess</a> <a href="/wiki/International_Grandmaster" class="mw-redirect" title="International Grandmaster">Grandmaster</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Karnam_Malleswari" title="Karnam Malleswari">Karnam Malleswari</a>, the first female Indian to win an <a href="/wiki/Olympic_medal" title="Olympic medal">Olympic medal</a>, hails from <a href="/wiki/Srikakulam_district" title="Srikakulam district">Srikakulam district</a> of Andhra Pradesh. She won the bronze medal on 19 September 2000, in the 69&#160;kg category with a lift of 240&#160;kg.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Krishnam_Raju_Gadiraju" title="Krishnam Raju Gadiraju">Krishnam Raju Gadiraju</a> of <a href="/wiki/Bhimavaram" title="Bhimavaram">Bhimavaram</a>, Andhra Pradesh, is a four-time world record holder. He is a <a href="/wiki/Speedcubing" title="Speedcubing">speedsolver</a> and <a href="/wiki/Unicycle" title="Unicycle">Unicyclist</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Pullela_Gopichand" title="Pullela Gopichand">Pullela Gopichand</a> is a former <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Badminton" title="Badminton">badminton</a> player. He won the <a href="/wiki/All_England_Open_Badminton_Championships" title="All England Open Badminton Championships">All England Open Badminton Championships</a> in 2001, becoming the second Indian to win after <a href="/wiki/Prakash_Padukone" title="Prakash Padukone">Prakash Padukone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mapsofindia_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mapsofindia-192">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-toi_dec02_193-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-toi_dec02-193">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GBA_194-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GBA-194">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Cherukuri_Lenin" title="Cherukuri Lenin">Cherukuri Lenin</a> (1985 or 1986 – 24 October 2010) was an Indian archer and coach who won a silver medal at the Asian Grand Prix in Malaysia, and was a national archery coach.
</p>
